guides</h1><div class="flex flex-row gap-2 items-center"><button class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg>Copy Markdown</button><button type="button" tabindex="0" data-base-ui-click-trigger="" id="base-ui-_R_t37lfivpfiv9db_" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring border bg-fd-secondary text-fd-secondary-foreground hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground px-2 py-1.5 text-xs gap-2">Open<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-chevron-down size-3.5 text-fd-muted-foreground" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m6 9 6 6 6-6"></path></svg></button></div></div><p class="mb-2 text-lg text-fd-muted-foreground">Learn how to write clear, consistent, and helpful guides for Prisma documentation</p><div class="prose flex-1"><h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="introduction"><a data-card="" href="#introduction" class="peer">Introduction</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>This guide shows you how to write guides for Prisma ORM documentation. It covers the required structure, formatting, and style conventions to ensure consistency across all guides. You&#x27;ll learn about frontmatter requirements, section organization, and writing style.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="prerequisites"><a data-card="" href="#prerequisites" class="peer">Prerequisites</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>Before writing a guide, make sure you have:</p>
<ul>
<li>A clear understanding of the topic you&#x27;re writing about</li>
<li>Access to the Prisma documentation repository</li>
<li>Familiarity with Markdown and MDX</li>
<li>Knowledge of the target audience for your guide</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="guide-structure"><a data-card="" href="#guide-structure" class="peer">Guide structure</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="required-frontmatter"><a data-card="" href="#required-frontmatter" class="peer">Required frontmatter</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Every guide must include the following frontmatter at the top of the file:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">---</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&#x27;[Descriptive title]&#x27;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">description</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&#x27;[One-sentence summary of what the guide covers]&#x27;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">---</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<ul>
<li><code>title</code>: A clear, descriptive title (e.g., &quot;Next.js&quot;, &quot;Multiple databases&quot;, &quot;GitHub Actions&quot;)</li>
<li><code>description</code>: A one-sentence summary that describes what you&#x27;ll learn or accomplish</li>
<li><code>image</code>: A unique header image for social media sharing (coordinate with the design team)</li>
</ul>
<p>All frontmatter fields should use sentence case.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="required-sections"><a data-card="" href="#required-sections" class="peer">Required sections</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong>Introduction</strong> (H2: <code>##</code>)</p>
<ul>
<li>Brief overview of what the guide covers</li>
<li>What the reader will learn/accomplish</li>
<li>Link to any example repositories or related resources on GitHub</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Prerequisites</strong> (H2: <code>##</code>)</p>
<ul>
<li>Required software/tools with version numbers (e.g., &quot;Node.js 20+&quot;)</li>
<li>Required accounts (e.g., &quot;A Prisma Data Platform account&quot;)</li>
<li>Keep it concise - only list what&#x27;s truly necessary</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Main content sections</strong> (H2: <code>##</code>)</p>
<ul>
<li>Use numbered steps (e.g., &quot;## 1. Set up your project&quot;, &quot;## 2. Install and Configure Prisma&quot;)</li>
<li>Use numbered subsections (e.g., &quot;### 2.1. Install dependencies&quot;, &quot;### 2.2. Define your Prisma Schema&quot;)</li>
<li>Each step should build on previous steps</li>
<li>Include all commands and code snippets needed</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Next steps</strong> (H2: <code>##</code>)</p>
<ul>
<li>What to do after completing the guide</li>
<li>Related guides or documentation (with links)</li>
<li>Additional resources</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="writing-style-and-voice"><a data-card="" href="#writing-style-and-voice" class="peer">Writing style and voice</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="general-principles"><a data-card="" href="#general-principles" class="peer">General principles</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<ul>
<li>Write in a clear, conversational tone</li>
<li>Use active voice and present tense</li>
<li>Address the reader directly using &quot;you&quot; (e.g., &quot;You&#x27;ll learn how to...&quot;)</li>
<li>Avoid jargon and explain technical terms when necessary</li>
<li>Be concise but thorough</li>
<li>Guide readers step-by-step through the process</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="code-examples"><a data-card="" href="#code-examples" class="peer">Code examples</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<ul>
<li>Include complete, runnable code examples</li>
<li>Use syntax highlighting with language specification</li>
<li>Include file paths in code block metadata using <code>title=</code></li>
<li>Use <code>// [!code ++]</code> to highlight added lines</li>
<li>Use <code>// [!code --]</code> to highlight removed lines</li>
<li>Use comments sparingly - only when needed to explain complex logic</li>
<li>Use <code>```npm</code> for package manager commands (auto-converts to pnpm/yarn/bun)</li>
<li>Use <code>```bash</code> for shell commands</li>
<li>Use <code>```text</code> for plain text files like <code>.env</code></li>
<li>Use <code>```typescript</code>, <code>```prisma</code>, <code>```json</code> for respective languages</li>
</ul>
<p>Example with file path:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="flex text-fd-muted-foreground items-center gap-2 h-9.5 border-b px-4"><div class="[&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M1.125 0C.502 0 0 .502 0 1.125v21.75C0 23.498.502 24 1.125 24h21.75c.623 0 1.125-.502 1.125-1.125V1.125C24 .502 23.498 0 22.875 0zm17.363 1.266.628.374.222.695.473.963.753.268.279.472.598.614.957.142.359.214.776.214 1.253 0 .657-.125 1.21-.373 1.656a3.033 3.033 0 0 1-1.012 1.085 4.38 4.38 0 0 1-1.487.596c-.566.12-1.163.18-1.79.18a9.916 0 0-.537-.5 5.597 5.597 0 0 0-.807-.444 27.72 27.72 0 0 0-1.007-.436c-.918-.383-1.602-.852-2.053-1.405-.45-.553-.676-1.222-.676-2.005 0-.614.123-1.141.369-1.582.246-.441.58-.804 1.004-1.089a4.494 4.494 0 0 1 1.47-.629 7.536 7.536 0 0 1 1.77-.201zm-15.113.188h9.563v2.166H9.506v9.646H6.789v-9.646H3.375z" fill="currentColor" /></svg></div><figcaption class="flex-1 <span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { PrismaPg } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;@prisma/adapter-pg&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> adapter</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> PrismaPg</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  connectionString: process.env.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">DATABASE_URL</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">!</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> prisma</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> PrismaClient</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  adapter,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">export</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> default</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> prisma;</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>

add"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;dotenv/config&quot;</span><span <h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="formatting-conventions"><a data-card="" href="#formatting-conventions" class="peer">Formatting conventions</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<ul>
<li>Use backticks for inline code:<!-- -->
<ul>
<li>File names: <code>`schema.prisma`</code></li>
<li>Directory names: <code>`prisma/`</code></li>
<li>Code elements: <code>`PrismaClient`</code></li>
<li>Package manager commands: Use <code>```npm</code> blocks (see <a href="#package-manager-commands">Package manager commands</a>)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Use admonitions for important information:<!-- -->
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:::info</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Context or background information</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:::</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:::note</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Important details to remember</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:::</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:::warning</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Critical information or gotchas</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:::</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:::tip</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Helpful suggestions or best practices</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:::</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
</li>
<li>Use proper heading hierarchy (never skip levels)</li>
<li>Use numbered sections (e.g., &quot;## 1. Setup&quot;, &quot;### 1.1. Install&quot;)</li>
<li>Link to other documentation pages using relative paths (e.g., <code>[Database drivers](/orm/core-concepts/supported-databases/database-drivers)</code>)</li>
</ul>

<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="common-patterns"><a data-card="" href="#common-patterns" class="peer">Common patterns</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="package-manager-commands"><a data-card="" href="#package-manager-commands" class="peer">Package manager commands</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Use <code>```npm</code> code blocks for package manager commands. These automatically convert to other package managers (pnpm, yarn, bun) in the UI:</p>
<div dir="ltr" data-orientation="horizontal" class="bg-background-default rounded-square border border-stroke-neutral overflow-hidden my-4"><div role="tablist" aria-orientation="horizontal" class="flex flex-row px-2 overflow-x-auto text-fd-muted-foreground bg-background-default" tabindex="-1" data-orientation="horizontal" style="outline:none"><button type="button" role="tab" aria-selected="true" aria-controls="radix-_R_tp7lfivpfiv9db_-content-npm" data-state="active" id="radix-_R_tp7lfivpfiv9db_-trigger-npm" class="relative group inline-flex text-sm font-medium text-nowrap items-center transition-colors gap-2 px-2 py-1.5 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-[state=active]:text-fd-primary [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5" tabindex="-1" data-orientation="horizontal" data-radix-collection-item=""><div class="absolute inset-x-2 bottom-0 h-px group-data-[state=active]:bg-fd-primary"></div>npm</button><button type="button" role="tab" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="radix-_R_tp7lfivpfiv9db_-content-pnpm" data-state="inactive" id="radix-_R_tp7lfivpfiv9db_-trigger-pnpm" class="relative group inline-flex text-sm font-medium text-nowrap items-center <h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="database-provider-compatibility"><a data-card="" href="#database-provider-compatibility" class="peer">Database provider compatibility</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Include an info admonition when commands or code are PostgreSQL-specific:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:::info</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">If you are using a different database provider (MySQL, SQL Server, SQLite), install the corresponding driver adapter package instead of </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`@prisma/adapter-pg`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">. For more information, see [</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-light-text-decoration:underline;--shiki-dark:#DBEDFF;--shiki-dark-text-decoration:underline">Database drivers</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">](</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-text-decoration:underline;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-text-decoration:underline">/orm/core-concepts/supported-databases/database-drivers</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">).</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:::</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>

<p>Include a warning about connection pooling:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:::warning</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">We recommend using a connection pooler (like [</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-light-text-decoration:underline;--shiki-dark:#DBEDFF;--shiki-dark-text-decoration:underline">Prisma Accelerate</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">](</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-text-decoration:underline;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-text-decoration:underline">https://www.prisma.io/accelerate</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)) to manage database connections efficiently.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:::</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="best-practices"><a data-card="" href="#best-practices" class="peer">Best practices</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong>Keep it focused</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Each guide should cover one main topic</li>
<li>Break complex topics into multiple guides</li>
<li>Link to related guides instead of duplicating content</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Show don&#x27;t tell</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Include practical, real-world examples</li>
<li>Provide complete, working code samples</li>
<li>Explain why certain approaches are recommended</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Consider the context</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Explain prerequisites clearly</li>
<li>Don&#x27;t assume prior knowledge</li>
<li>Link to foundational concepts within or outside of our docs when needed</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Maintain consistency</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Follow the established guide structure</li>
<li>Use consistent terminology</li>
<li>Match the style of existing guides</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Think about maintenance</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Use version numbers where appropriate</li>
<li>Avoid time-sensitive references</li>
<li>Consider future updates when structuring content</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="guide-template"><a data-card="" href="#guide-template" class="peer">Guide template</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>Use this template as a starting point for new guides. The template includes common sections and patterns used across Prisma guides.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="basic-template-structure"><a data-card="" href="#basic-template-structure" class="peer">Basic template structure</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Copy this template for a new guide:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">---</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&#x27;[Your guide title]&#x27;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">description</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&#x27;[One-sentence summary of what you&#x27;ll learn]&#x27;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">image</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&#x27;/img/guides/[guide-name]-cover.png&#x27;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">---</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## Introduction</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">[Brief overview of what this guide covers and what you&#x27;ll accomplish. Include a link to an example repository if available.]</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## Prerequisites</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> [</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-light-text-decoration:underline;--shiki-dark:#DBEDFF;--shiki-dark-text-decoration:underline">Node.js 20+</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">](</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-text-decoration:underline;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-text-decoration:underline">https://nodejs.org</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> [Any other prerequisites]</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## 1. Set up your project</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">[Instructions for creating or setting up the project]</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```npm</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"># Example command</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">npx create-next-app@latest my-app</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">cd my-app</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## 2. Install and Configure Prisma</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">### 2.1. Install dependencies</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">To get started with Prisma, you&#x27;ll need to install a few dependencies:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```npm</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">npm install prisma tsx @types/pg --save-dev</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```npm</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">npm install @prisma/client @prisma/adapter-pg dotenv pg</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:::info</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">If you are using a different database provider (MySQL, SQL Server, SQLite), install the corresponding driver adapter package instead of </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`@prisma/adapter-pg`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">. For more information, see [</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-light-text-decoration:underline;--shiki-dark:#DBEDFF;--shiki-dark-text-decoration:underline">Database drivers</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">](</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-text-decoration:underline;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-text-decoration:underline">/orm/core-concepts/supported-databases/database-drivers</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">).</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:::</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Once installed, initialize Prisma in your project:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```npm</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">npx prisma init --db --output ../generated/prisma</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:::info</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">You&#x27;ll need to answer a few questions while setting up your Prisma Postgres database. Select the region closest to your location and a memorable name for your database.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:::</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">This will create:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> A </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`prisma`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> directory with a </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`schema.prisma`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> file</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> A Prisma Postgres database</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> A </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`.env`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> file containing the </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`DATABASE_URL`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> A </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`prisma.config.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> file for configuration</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">### 2.2. Define your Prisma Schema</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">In the </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`prisma/schema.prisma`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> file, add your models:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```prisma title=&quot;prisma/schema.prisma&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">generator client {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  provider = &quot;prisma-client&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  output   = &quot;../generated/prisma&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">datasource db {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  provider = &quot;postgresql&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">model User { // [!code ++]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id    Int     @id @default(autoincrement()) // [!code ++]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  email String  @unique // [!code ++]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  name  String? // [!code ++]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  posts Post[] // [!code ++]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">} // [!code ++]</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">model Post { // [!code ++]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id        Int     @id @default(autoincrement()) // [!code ++]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  title     String // [!code ++]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  content   String? // [!code ++]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  published Boolean @default(false) // [!code ++]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  authorId  Int // [!code ++]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  author    User    @relation(fields: [authorId], references: [id]) // [!code ++]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">} // [!code ++]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">### 2.3. Run migrations and generate Prisma Client</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Create the database tables:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```npm</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">npx prisma migrate dev --name init</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Then generate Prisma Client:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```npm</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">npx prisma generate</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## 3. [Integration-specific steps]</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">[Add framework or platform-specific integration steps here]</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## Next steps</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Now that you&#x27;ve completed this guide, you can:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> [Suggestion 1]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> [Suggestion 2]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> [</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-light-text-decoration:underline;--shiki-dark:#DBEDFF;--shiki-dark-text-decoration:underline">Related guide 1</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">](</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-text-decoration:underline;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-text-decoration:underline">/path/to/guide</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> [</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-light-text-decoration:underline;--shiki-dark:#DBEDFF;--shiki-dark-text-decoration:underline">Related guide 2</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">](</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-text-decoration:underline;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-text-decoration:underline">/path/to/guide</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">For more information:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> [</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-light-text-decoration:underline;--shiki-dark:#DBEDFF;--shiki-dark-text-decoration:underline">Prisma documentation</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">](</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-text-decoration:underline;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-text-decoration:underline">/orm</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> [Related documentation]</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="adding-guides-to-navigation"><a data-card="" href="#adding-guides-to-navigation" class="peer">Adding guides to navigation</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>Guides are organized by category in subdirectories. To add a guide to the navigation, you need to update the appropriate <code>meta.json</code> file.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="main-categories"><a data-card="" href="#main-categories" class="peer">Main categories</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>The main guide categories are listed in <code>meta.json</code>:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" <span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">  &quot;title&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;Guides&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">  &quot;root&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">true</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">  &quot;icon&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;NotebookTabs&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>

<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="adding-a-guide-to-a-category"><a data-card="" href="#adding-a-guide-to-a-category" class="peer">Adding a guide to a category</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>To add a guide to a category (e.g., <code>frameworks</code>), edit the category&#x27;s <code>meta.json</code> file:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark has-diff" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="flex text-fd-muted-foreground items-center gap-2 h-9.5 border-b px-4"><div class="[&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M 6,1 C 4.354992,1 3,2.354992 3,4 v 16 c 0,1.645008 1.354992,3 3,3 h 12 c 1.645008,0 3,-1.354992 3,-3 V 8 7 A 1.0001,1.0001 0 0 0 20.707031,6.2929687 l -5,-5 A 1.0001,1.0001 0 0 0 15,1 h -1 z m 0,2 h 7 v 3 c 0,1.645008 1.354992,3 3,3 h 3 v 11 c 0,0.564129 -0.435871,1 -1,1 H 6 C 5.4358712,21 5,20.564129 5,20 V 4 C 5,3.4358712 5.4358712,3 6,3 Z M 15,3.4140625 18.585937,7 H 16 C 15.435871,7 15,6.5641288 15,6 Z" fill="currentColor" /></svg></div><figcaption class="flex-1 truncate">apps/docs/content/docs/guides/frameworks/meta.json</figcaption><div class="empty:hidden -me-2"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">{</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">  &quot;title&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;Frameworks&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">  &quot;defaultOpen&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">true</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">  &quot;pages&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: [</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">    &quot;nextjs&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">    &quot;astro&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">    &quot;nuxt&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line diff add"><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">    &quot;your-new-guide&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  ]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>The page name should match your <code>.mdx</code> filename without the extension. For example, if your file is <code>your-new-guide.mdx</code>, add <code>&quot;your-new-guide&quot;</code> to the <code>pages</code> array.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="next-steps"><a data-card="" href="#next-steps" class="peer">Next steps</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>After reading this guide, you can:</p>
<ul>
<li>Start writing your own guide using the provided template</li>
<li>Review existing guides in the category you&#x27;re contributing to</li>
<li>Coordinate with the design team for a unique header image</li>
<li>Submit your guide for review</li>
</ul></div><div class="flex flex-row flex-wrap items-center justify-between gap-4 border-t pt-6 text-sm"><a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener"
